Subject: FW: GT students and advanced classes

 

Parents,

 

I was made aware that several of your students were not placed in the
advanced classes. As identified gifted students, they have the right to be
placed in all advanced classes. If you do not want them placed, you can
sign a waiver to have them removed them from the class. 

 

I have been in contact with Pattie Tribble and Anthony Thompson at the
middle school about this. Mr. Thompson will fix this issue in June. Please
send him an email stating that your child is in ACE and was not assigned
to AP ________. I am forwarding the emails that have been exchanged so you
can see how the issue will be addressed. Let me know if you have
questions. 

 

I will miss your sweet children dearly!

 

 

Cindy Thompson

Gifted Education Specialist
Monrovia Elementary School

Phone  256-851-4570

Fax  256-851-4571

 

"If you are continually asked to jump over a bar that requires little
effort, how long will it be before that's as high as you can jump?" ~
Carol Ann Tomlinson

Subject: GT students and advanced classes

 

Pattie,

 

Several of my 5th grade students' parents have told me that their children
are not in all of the AP classes at MMS. The Gifted Specialists were told
a few years ago that since GT students are not directly serviced after
elementary school, they would be automatically placed in the AP classes
and parents would have the option to sign a waiver to remove their child
from a class or from all of the classes if they wanted to. The LEA reads
as follows.

 

 



 



 



 

Some of these parents are quite upset about their children not being in
the classes. Could you help with this? I'm forwarding the list of upcoming
6th grade students' names that I sent on May 12 to help you check their
schedules. Please let me know what will be done so I can inform the
parents. 

 

Thanks!

 

 

Cindy Thompson

Gifted Education Specialist
